          --monorail-metadata-toggled-bg: var(--monorail-metadata-closed-bg);
        }

          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: flex-start;
          z-index: 200;

          flex-grow: 1;

          flex-wrap: no-wrap;
        }

        }

          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);

          width: 100%;

        }

            width: 100%;

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

UserAgent: Mozilla/5.0 (X11; Linux x86_64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/92.0.4515.107 Safari/537.36



<span class="line"><!---->UserAgent: Mozilla/5.0 (X11; Linux x86_64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/92.0.4515.107 Safari/537.36<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Steps to reproduce the problem:



<span class="line"><!---->Steps to reproduce the problem:<!----></span>



<br>





1. apply the patch and compile chrome



<span class="line"><!---->1. apply the patch and compile chrome<!----></span>



<br>





2. start a server: `python -m SimpleHTTPServer 8605`



<span class="line"><!---->2. start a server: `python -m SimpleHTTPServer 8605`<!----></span>



<br>





3. ./chrome --incognito 



<span class="line"><!---->3. ./chrome --incognito <!----></span>





http://127.0.0.1:8605/poc.html



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="http://127.0.0.1:8605/poc.html"><!---->http://127.0.0.1:8605/poc.html<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





What is the expected behavior?



<span class="line"><!---->What is the expected behavior?<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





What went wrong?



<span class="line"><!---->What went wrong?<!----></span>



<br>





Chrome will use OffTheRecordProfileImpl in incognito mode. When ~OffTheRecordProfileImpl() [1]is called, it will call DestroyFactoriesInOrder()[2] to destroy the KeyedService, including ClientSideDetectionService.



<span class="line"><!---->Chrome will use OffTheRecordProfileImpl in incognito mode. When ~OffTheRecordProfileImpl() [1]is called, it will call DestroyFactoriesInOrder()[2] to destroy the KeyedService, including ClientSideDetectionService.<!----></span>



<br>





However, if we could close the browser before ClientSideDetectionService was added to the  `dependency_manager_`[3], there will still be a ClientSideDetectionService instance but  DestroyFactoriesInOrder() will not destroy it, because it was not in the  `destruction_order1`[4]. After ~OffTheRecordProfileImpl(), ClientSideDetectionServiceFactory will destruct ClientSideDetectionService, which will call ~PrefChangeRegistrar()[5] and use `PrefServiceSyncable` in function RemoveAll(). But `PrefServiceSyncable` has been deleted in ~OffTheRecordProfileImpl() => UAF occurs.



<span class="line"><!---->However, if we could close the browser before ClientSideDetectionService was added to the  `dependency_manager_`[3], there will still be a ClientSideDetectionService instance but  DestroyFactoriesInOrder() will not destroy it, because it was not in the  `destruction_order1`[4]. After ~OffTheRecordProfileImpl(), ClientSideDetectionServiceFactory will destruct ClientSideDetectionService, which will call ~PrefChangeRegistrar()[5] and use `PrefServiceSyncable` in function RemoveAll(). But `PrefServiceSyncable` has been deleted in ~OffTheRecordProfileImpl() =&gt; UAF occurs.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:components/prefs/pref_change_registrar.cc;l=23;drc=805a9df0b462c26bbd0b05dc69c6779483758176;bpv=0;bpt=0"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:components/prefs/pref_change_registrar.cc;l=23;drc=805a9df0b462c26bbd0b05dc69c6779483758176;bpv=0;bpt=0<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





It's difficult to reproduce this UAF because you cannot precisely control when the browser is closed. So I patch the code in `PerformInterlockedTwoPhaseShutdown` to simulate that ClientSideDetectionService is not in the `destruction_order1`. BTW, other keyedservices could also trigger this problem, I happen to reproduce it with HostContentSettingsMap without any patches. You can see the asan log for more information.



<span class="line"><!---->It's difficult to reproduce this UAF because you cannot precisely control when the browser is closed. So I patch the code in `PerformInterlockedTwoPhaseShutdown` to simulate that ClientSideDetectionService is not in the `destruction_order1`. BTW, other keyedservices could also trigger this problem, I happen to reproduce it with HostContentSettingsMap without any patches. You can see the asan log for more information.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

Taking the bug, I started looking into the code.

<br>





Another possible cause is that HostContentSettingsMap seems to delete its state in its destructor, whereas maybe it should do that in Shutdown(). This is especially important because HostContentSettingsMap is refcounted, so there's no guarantee that the profile is still alive at destruction.



<span class="line"><!---->Another possible cause is that HostContentSettingsMap seems to delete its state in its destructor, whereas maybe it should do that in Shutdown(). This is especially important because HostContentSettingsMap is refcounted, so there's no guarantee that the profile is still alive at destruction.<!----></span>

Noting my current observations here:



<span class="line"><!---->Noting my current observations here:<!----></span>



<br>





- the crash happens because a PolicyProvider in  HostContentSettingsMap::content_settings_providers_ is still holding a reference to profile when destroyed



<span class="line"><!---->- the crash happens because a PolicyProvider in  HostContentSettingsMap::content_settings_providers_ is still holding a reference to profile when destroyed<!----></span>



<br>





- PolicyProvider has the same lifetime as HostContentSettingsMap (constructed and destroyed at the same time, and also has a  ShutdownOnUIThread() method)



<span class="line"><!---->- PolicyProvider has the same lifetime as HostContentSettingsMap (constructed and destroyed at the same time, and also has a  ShutdownOnUIThread() method)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This would point to either ShutdownOnUIThread() 1) not being called or 2) not releasing the reference to the profile. However, so far I'm not seeing anything wrong in the code that would cause either of those.



<span class="line"><!---->This would point to either ShutdownOnUIThread() 1) not being called or 2) not releasing the reference to the profile. However, so far I'm not seeing anything wrong in the code that would cause either of those.<!----></span>

It is expected that HostContentSettingsMap can live longer than the Profile as it is still needed after shutdown of some other services. E.g. for cookie deletion on exit.



<span class="line"><!---->It is expected that HostContentSettingsMap can live longer than the Profile as it is still needed after shutdown of some other services. E.g. for cookie deletion on exit.<!----></span>



<br>





This means that HostContentSettingsMap and all of its providers drop all profile-related references in ShutdownOnUIThread(). The PolicyProvider does this as well and it also calls RemoveAll() on pref_change_registrar. So it is really weird that pref_change_registrar crashes when PolicyProvider is destroyed.



<span class="line"><!---->This means that HostContentSettingsMap and all of its providers drop all profile-related references in ShutdownOnUIThread(). The PolicyProvider does this as well and it also calls RemoveAll() on pref_change_registrar. So it is really weird that pref_change_registrar crashes when PolicyProvider is destroyed.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





If it is possible to create a HostContentSettingsMap after Profile shutdown, maybe we could detect this by adding some DCHECK into the HCSM constructor to ensure that it is not created for a dead Profile?



<span class="line"><!---->If it is possible to create a HostContentSettingsMap after Profile shutdown, maybe we could detect this by adding some DCHECK into the HCSM constructor to ensure that it is not created for a dead Profile?<!----></span>

Hi, if you still can't repro that, maybe you can download the userdata.zip and use it as the `--user-data-dir`



<span class="line"><!---->Hi, if you still can't repro that, maybe you can download the userdata.zip and use it as the `--user-data-dir`<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Step:



<span class="line"><!---->Step:<!----></span>



<br>





1. download asan-linux-release-939207.zip  and unzip



<span class="line"><!---->1. download asan-linux-release-939207.zip  and unzip<!----></span>



<br>





2. `mkdir out` and copy `poc.html` and `copy_mojo_js_bindings.py` to `out`.



<span class="line"><!---->2. `mkdir out` and copy `poc.html` and `copy_mojo_js_bindings.py` to `out`.<!----></span>



<br>





3.  cd to `out` and `python copy_mojo_js_bindings.py /path/to/asan-linux-release-939207/gen/`



<span class="line"><!---->3.  cd to `out` and `python copy_mojo_js_bindings.py /path/to/asan-linux-release-939207/gen/`<!----></span>



<br>





4. start a http server at `out` :  `python -m SimpleHTTPServer 8605`



<span class="line"><!---->4. start a http server at `out` :  `python -m SimpleHTTPServer 8605`<!----></span>



<br>





5. unzip userdata.zip to get `noexist` directory.



<span class="line"><!---->5. unzip userdata.zip to get `noexist` directory.<!----></span>



<br>





6. ./chrome --enable-blink-features=MojoJS    --user-data-dir=/PATH/TO/noexist  



<span class="line"><!---->6. ./chrome --enable-blink-features=MojoJS    --user-data-dir=/PATH/TO/noexist  <!----></span>

Hi, after debugging this problem, I finally find a simple poc that can easily trigger this UAF. 



<span class="line"><!---->Hi, after debugging this problem, I finally find a simple poc that can easily trigger this UAF. <!----></span>



<br>





Repo:



<span class="line"><!---->Repo:<!----></span>



<br>





1. download asan-linux-release-955038.zip and unzip



<span class="line"><!---->1. download asan-linux-release-955038.zip and unzip<!----></span>



<br>





2. at the folder of poc.html create a file:  `touch no.js`  and start a server: 1python -m SimpleHTTPServer 86051



<span class="line"><!---->2. at the folder of poc.html create a file:  `touch no.js`  and start a server: 1python -m SimpleHTTPServer 86051<!----></span>



<br>





3. ./chrome --user-data-dir=/tmp/noexist 



<span class="line"><!---->3. ./chrome --user-data-dir=/tmp/noexist <!----></span>





http://127.0.0.1:8605/poc.html



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="http://127.0.0.1:8605/poc.html"><!---->http://127.0.0.1:8605/poc.html<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





And I also find a root cause:



<span class="line"><!---->And I also find a root cause:<!----></span>



<br>





~ProfileImpl() will call ShutdownStoragePartitions()[1], and it will finally create another `HostContentSettingsMapFactory`[2]. `HostContentSettingsMapFactory` is a keyed_service, so it was created at the beginning of chrome firstly. Now we have two  `HostContentSettingsMapFactory` . ~ProfileImpl() will delete one and when another one is destructed, UAF occurs.



<span class="line"><!---->~ProfileImpl() will call ShutdownStoragePartitions()[1], and it will finally create another `HostContentSettingsMapFactory`[2]. `HostContentSettingsMapFactory` is a keyed_service, so it was created at the beginning of chrome firstly. Now we have two  `HostContentSettingsMapFactory` . ~ProfileImpl() will delete one and when another one is destructed, UAF occurs.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Specifically, `HostContentSettingsMapFactory` will create a `HostContentSettingsMap`, `HostContentSettingsMap` has member `std::map<ProviderType,std::unique_ptr<content_settings::ProviderInterface>>   content_settings_providers_;`. The value of this map is `ProviderInterface`, the actual class used there is `PolicyProvider`. `PolicyProvider` has a member `PrefChangeRegistrar pref_change_registrar_;`, `PrefChangeRegistrar ` has a member `service_`, this `service_` is a raw pointer created by `CreateSyncable`[3], `CreateSyncable` will create a unique_ptr owned by `ProfileImpl`, and `service_` is assigned with unique_ptr.get(). So after ~ProfileImpl(), this unique_ptr is reset and `service_` is also deleted. When we destruct seond `HostContentSettingsMap`, this `service_` is used again => UAF. This explains why ASAN report like this.



<span class="line"><!---->Specifically, `HostContentSettingsMapFactory` will create a `HostContentSettingsMap`, `HostContentSettingsMap` has member `std::map&lt;ProviderType,std::unique_ptr&lt;content_settings::ProviderInterface&gt;&gt;   content_settings_providers_;`. The value of this map is `ProviderInterface`, the actual class used there is `PolicyProvider`. `PolicyProvider` has a member `PrefChangeRegistrar pref_change_registrar_;`, `PrefChangeRegistrar ` has a member `service_`, this `service_` is a raw pointer created by `CreateSyncable`[3], `CreateSyncable` will create a unique_ptr owned by `ProfileImpl`, and `service_` is assigned with unique_ptr.get(). So after ~ProfileImpl(), this unique_ptr is reset and `service_` is also deleted. When we destruct seond `HostContentSettingsMap`, this `service_` is used again =&gt; UAF. This explains why ASAN report like this.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>





I provide the call stack when `HostContentSettingsMapFactory` is called the second time, we could infer that `payment` and `service worker` could create another `HostContentSettingsMapFactory`. So my poc uses a service worker and payment API.



<span class="line"><!---->I provide the call stack when `HostContentSettingsMapFactory` is called the second time, we could infer that `payment` and `service worker` could create another `HostContentSettingsMapFactory`. So my poc uses a service worker and payment API.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:chrome/browser/profiles/profile_impl.cc;l=926;drc=45dc15e901ba2d7ca5549c9551ccb1cb3f6f9ec5;bpv=1;bpt=0"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:chrome/browser/profiles/profile_impl.cc;l=926;drc=45dc15e901ba2d7ca5549c9551ccb1cb3f6f9ec5;bpv=1;bpt=0<!----></a>

Thanks for the improved test case. I can reproduce the issue! 



<span class="line"><!---->Thanks for the improved test case. I can reproduce the issue! <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





In debug builds, there is actually a NOTREACHED() that gets triggered when we attempt to create a service after profile shutdown: 



<span class="line"><!---->In debug builds, there is actually a NOTREACHED() that gets triggered when we attempt to create a service after profile shutdown: <!----></span>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:components/keyed_service/core/dependency_manager.cc;l=169;drc=bd1b0b6a99ed26149b2a9ec1e2c75f9e499b31f9



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:components/keyed_service/core/dependency_manager.cc;l=169;drc=bd1b0b6a99ed26149b2a9ec1e2c75f9e499b31f9"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:components/keyed_service/core/dependency_manager.cc;l=169;drc=bd1b0b6a99ed26149b2a9ec1e2c75f9e499b31f9<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





In release builds, this only triggers a silent crash report. Maybe we should just put a hard CHECK() here to avoid any potential use-after-free?



<span class="line"><!---->In release builds, this only triggers a silent crash report. Maybe we should just put a hard CHECK() here to avoid any potential use-after-free?<!----></span>



<br>





This only seems to happen very rarely in real usage: 



<span class="line"><!---->This only seems to happen very rarely in real usage: <!----></span>





http://crash/browse?q=product_name%3D%27Chrome%27+AND+product.Version%3E%3D%2796.%27+AND+EXISTS+%28SELECT+1+FROM+UNNEST%28CrashedStackTrace.StackFrame%29+WHERE+FunctionName%3D%27DependencyManager%3A%3AAssertContextWasntDestroyed%28void+*%29%27%29#+samplereports,productname:1000,productversion:50,magicsignature:50,magicsignature2:50,stablesignature:50,clientid:20,url:30,simplifiedurl:30,experiments:1000,country:30



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="http://crash/browse?q=product_name%3D%27Chrome%27+AND+product.Version%3E%3D%2796.%27+AND+EXISTS+%28SELECT+1+FROM+UNNEST%28CrashedStackTrace.StackFrame%29+WHERE+FunctionName%3D%27DependencyManager%3A%3AAssertContextWasntDestroyed%28void+*%29%27%29#+samplereports,productname:1000,productversion:50,magicsignature:50,magicsignature2:50,stablesignature:50,clientid:20,url:30,simplifiedurl:30,experiments:1000,country:30"><!---->http://crash/browse?q=product_name%3D%27Chrome%27+AND+product.Version%3E%3D%2796.%27+AND+EXISTS+%28SELECT+1+FROM+UNNEST%28CrashedStackTrace.StackFrame%29+WHERE+FunctionName%3D%27DependencyManager%3A%3AAssertContextWasntDestroyed%28void+*%29%27%29#+samplereports,productname:1000,productversion:50,magicsignature:50,magicsignature2:50,stablesignature:50,clientid:20,url:30,simplifiedurl:30,experiments:1000,country:30<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





For the cases that access a HostContentSettingsMap after shutdown, we should ensure that they obtain a scoped_refptr before shutdown is started. This will ensure that HostContentSettingsMap is not created again.



<span class="line"><!---->For the cases that access a HostContentSettingsMap after shutdown, we should ensure that they obtain a scoped_refptr before shutdown is started. This will ensure that HostContentSettingsMap is not created again.<!----></span>

Comment

 to turn a potential use-after-free into a clean crash:

PaymentAppDatabase::DidReadAllPaymentInstruments seems to be triggered by a WrapCallbackWithDefaultInvokeIfNotRun. This triggers the callback on shutdown.



<span class="line"><!---->PaymentAppDatabase::DidReadAllPaymentInstruments seems to be triggered by a WrapCallbackWithDefaultInvokeIfNotRun. This triggers the callback on shutdown.<!----></span>



<br>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:content/browser/service_worker/service_worker_registry.cc;l=687;drc=bd1b0b6a99ed26149b2a9ec1e2c75f9e499b31f9



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:content/browser/service_worker/service_worker_registry.cc;l=687;drc=bd1b0b6a99ed26149b2a9ec1e2c75f9e499b31f9"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:content/browser/service_worker/service_worker_registry.cc;l=687;drc=bd1b0b6a99ed26149b2a9ec1e2c75f9e499b31f9<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





The callback passes an error but PaymentAppDatabase::DidReadAllPaymentInstruments still calls its callback.



<span class="line"><!---->The callback passes an error but PaymentAppDatabase::DidReadAllPaymentInstruments still calls its callback.<!----></span>

Date: Mon Jan 10 14:56:57 2022



<span class="line"><!---->Date: Mon Jan 10 14:56:57 2022<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Prevent use-after-free if a KeyedService is accessed after shutdown



<span class="line"><!---->Prevent use-after-free if a KeyedService is accessed after shutdown<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





KeyedServices should not get created during shutdown. This is prevented



<span class="line"><!---->KeyedServices should not get created during shutdown. This is prevented<!----></span>



<br>





in debug builds by a NOTREACHED() but only leads to a silent crash



<span class="line"><!---->in debug builds by a NOTREACHED() but only leads to a silent crash<!----></span>



<br>





report in release builds. Considering that this can lead to security



<span class="line"><!---->report in release builds. Considering that this can lead to security<!----></span>



<br>





bugs, we should have a hard CHECK(false) to prevent services from being



<span class="line"><!---->bugs, we should have a hard CHECK(false) to prevent services from being<!----></span>



<br>





created during shutdown.



<span class="line"><!---->created during shutdown.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

<br>





window was shutting down, the payment apps would still be sent for

<br>





permission checks, causing a crash.



<span class="line"><!---->permission checks, causing a crash.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





After the change, in the same situation, the payment apps would not be



<span class="line"><!---->After the change, in the same situation, the payment apps would not be<!----></span>



<br>





sent for permission checks.



<span class="line"><!---->sent for permission checks.<!----></span>

[M98] Not to send Payment apps for permission check when service worker errors



<span class="line"><!---->[M98] Not to send Payment apps for permission check when service worker errors<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Before the change, when a payment app was being registered while the



<span class="line"><!---->Before the change, when a payment app was being registered while the<!----></span>



<br>





window was shutting down, the payment apps would still be sent for



<span class="line"><!---->window was shutting down, the payment apps would still be sent for<!----></span>



<br>





permission checks, causing a crash.



<span class="line"><!---->permission checks, causing a crash.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





After the change, in the same situation, the payment apps would not be



<span class="line"><!---->After the change, in the same situation, the payment apps would not be<!----></span>



<br>





sent for permission checks.



<span class="line"><!---->sent for permission checks.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

It appears that this triggering this UAF requires browser shutdown and can only be triggered if the website itself is able to initiate that browser shutdown, which is reliant on starting Chrome with the website as an argument. As this issue UAF is triggered upon browser shutdown it provides quite a bit less of attacker control to exploit, which is why the reward amount was decided at $7,000, which is consistent for browser UAF with this amount of mitigation.

 <script type="text/javascript" nonce="">
 window.addEventListener('load', () => {
 window.getTSMonClient().recordIssueDetailSpaTiming();
 });
 </script>

<script type="text/javascript" nonce="">
 runOnLoad(function() {
 if (typeof(ClientLogger) === "function") {
 let cl = new ClientLogger("issues");
 if (cl.started("new-issue")) {
 cl.logEnd("new-issue", null, 120 * 1000);
 }
 if (cl.started("issue-search")) {
 cl.logEnd("issue-search");
 }
 }
 });
</script>
